mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">Wildspace Encounters table</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">或</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">星界海遭遇表</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 16pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Regular; COLOR: rgb(0,106,190); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">Astral Sea Encounters table</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">来随机生成一个星界遭遇或者按照自己的心意直接选择</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 16pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">如果该遭遇有涉及到</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">魔法船</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">，你可以通过掷骰并对照</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">舰船</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">遭遇表</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 16pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Regular; COLOR: rgb(0,106,190); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">Ship Encounters table</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 16pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Regular; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"> </span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">来决定船的类型以及船员，或者你也可以自创一个属于你自己的</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">舰船</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">遭遇（</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">参见</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">《星界冒险者指南</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 16pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Regular; COLOR: rgb(0,106,190); FONT-STYLE: italic; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">Astral Adventurer's Guide</span>*<span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">》</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">来获得舰船的详述</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">）。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Regular; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">标有星号</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Bold; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">(\*)的生物</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">均</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Bold; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">出现在本书中；其余的</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">则</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Bold; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">在</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">《</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Bold; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">怪物图鉴</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">》</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Bold; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">中都有描述。任何带有匕首()标记的生物都可以</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">充当</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">法驱者</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Bold; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">，因为它是</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">一位</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Bold; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">施法者</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Bold; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Bold; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">如果一名类人生物不具有特定种族，它可以是你所选择的任何种族。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Bold; COLOR: rgb(36,37,39); mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 22pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 22pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">初始态度</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 22pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Regular; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">Initial Attitude</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 22pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Regular; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">根据遭遇表上的标记来掷态度骰，然后在初始态度表上进行对照以随机决定遭遇生物的初始态度。</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Regular; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"></span>

<span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">初始</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 14pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-ascii-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-hansi-font-family: Roboto-Regular; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'">态度</span>**<span style="FONT-SIZE: 16pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Bold; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体">Initial Attitude</span><span style="FONT-SIZE: 16pt; FONT-FAMILY: Roboto-Bold; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; mso-bidi-font-family: 'Times New Roman'; mso-font-kerning: 1.0000pt; mso-spacerun: 'yes'; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体"></span>**
